  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于语言的室内定位多停留在“找到是哪一处场景”的粗粒度级别，无法在同一场景内确定精确姿态。相机等视觉输入存在隐私与部署成本。作者希望仅凭自然语言，实现无需相机、轻量且隐私友好的精细定位。

Method: 提出LangLoc三阶段流水线：1) 场景检索：双分支GATv2编码器融合CLIP语义特征，提升语言-场景匹配；2) 位置与朝向估计：在地面网格上以光线投射计算物体可见性，基于与描述一致性为每个网格打分，得到2D位置与朝向；3) 残余歧义消解：贝叶斯对话模块提出有针对性的是/否问题，基于回答更新位姿后验直至收敛。并构建含13k+带位姿标注的语言描述、覆盖1300+室内3D扫描的基准。

Result: 场景检索Top-1召回率较SOTA提升8个百分点；位置-朝向回归中位误差约0.95米；通过交互式问答可进一步收敛到单一精确位置。

Conclusion: 自然语言可在无相机条件下实现实用的细粒度室内定位。LangLoc将检索、几何一致性估计与贝叶斯对话结合，显著提升精度与可用性，并提供新基准促进该方向研究。

Abstract: We tackle fine-grained indoor localization from natural language: given a free-form description of one's surroundings, estimate the observer's 2D position and heading within a known 3D environment. Language queries are lightweight, privacy-preserving, and need no camera - yet prior work stops at coarse scene retrieval and cannot resolve an intra-scene pose. We close this gap with LangLoc, a three-stage pipeline that (i) retrieves the correct scene via a dual-branch GATv2 encoder with CLIP semantic features, surpassing the previous best by 8 percentage points in Top-1 recall; (ii) estimates position and heading by scoring a dense floor grid through ray-cast object visibility, reaching a median error of 0.95 m; and (iii) resolves residual ambiguity through a Bayesian dialog module that asks targeted yes/no questions and updates a pose posterior until the location is pinpointed. To support this task we contribute a benchmark of $13{,}000{+}$ pose-indexed natural-language descriptions over $1{,}300{+}$ indoor 3D scans.

</details>


### [287] [RADIANCE: Relative Adaptive Denoising with IP-Adapter for Novel Concept Enhancement](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05088)
*Zi-Xiang Ni,Bo-Lun Huang,Teng-Fang Hsiao,Bo-Kai Ruan,Hong-Han Shuai*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: RADIANCE 是一个无需再训练的推理期闭环反馈框架，借助监测-调控-调度三件套与多对象扩展策略，显著提升T2I扩散模型对稀有“属性-对象”组合的构图平衡与对齐，同时保持接近原生延迟。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有T2I扩散模型在罕见组合（如非常见属性-对象配对）上易出现遗漏或语义漂移，被主导实体“带偏”。根因在于去噪轨迹缺乏组合层面的平衡与纠偏机制，因此需要在不再训练的前提下，于推理过程中动态监测并校正组合对齐。

Method: 提出 RADIANCE，将推理视为闭环反馈：
1) 组合相似度监测（CSM）：用CLIP度量中间潜变量中对象与属性的出现强度，提供反馈信号；
2) 双向尺度控制（BSC）：利用正/负 IP-Adapter scale 施加“恢复力”，对偏向的轨迹实时再平衡；
3) 反馈引导调度（FGS）：在时间步上协调监测与控制，无需额外训练。
多对象扩展：
- 延迟适配器激活（DAA）避免过早融合；
- 分层交替引导（LAG）在层级上交替施加引导，减轻概念混叠。
并行流水：监测与去噪重叠执行以维持低延迟。

Result: 在 RareBench 与 T2I-CompBench 上，RADIANCE 提升了组合对齐度与感知质量；提升的是“每样本成功率”和有效吞吐量，同时与SOTA基线相比保持竞争性的推理时延。

Conclusion: 通过在推理期引入闭环反馈和可插拔模块，RADIANCE 无需再训练即可稳健缓解稀有组合的遗漏与语义漂移问题，在多对象场景同样有效，并在质量-效率上取得兼顾。

Abstract: Text-to-image (T2I) diffusion models have achieved striking progress but still struggle to synthesize rare concepts involving unusual attribute-object pairings, often resulting in concept omission or semantic drift where a dominant entity overwhelms the generation. Tracing these failures to a lack of compositional balance during the denoising trajectory, we propose RADIANCE, a training-free framework that treats inference as a closed-loop feedback process. RADIANCE augments pretrained backbones with three modular components: (1) a Compositional Similarity Monitor (CSM) that tracks the emergence of objects and attributes in intermediate latents via CLIP-based feedback; (2) a Bidirectional Scale Controller (BSC) that applies a reactive "restoring force" using positive and negative IP-Adapter scales to rebalance biased trajectories; and (3) a Feedback Guidance Scheduler (FGS) that coordinates these updates across timesteps without additional training. We further extend the framework to multi-object prompts via Delayed Adapter Activation (DAA) and Layer-wise Alternating Guidance (LAG) to prevent premature concept fusion. By overlapping monitoring and denoising through pipelined execution, RADIANCE maintains competitive latency while significantly enhancing the per-sample success rate and effective throughput. Experiments on RareBench and T2I-CompBench demonstrate that RADIANCE consistently enhances compositional alignment and perceptual quality over state-of-the-art baselines.

### [288] [TimeThink: Reasoning with Time for Video LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05089)
*Handong Li,Longteng Guo,Zikang Liu,Dongze Hao,Yepeng Tang,Zijia Zhao,Jie Jiang,Zhiwei Jin,Chen Chen,Haonan Lu,Jing Liu*

TL;DR: TimeThink提出一种面向视频推理的强化学习框架，将“时间线索”作为逐步优化单元，通过步级时间过程奖励与结果奖励的联合目标，显式引导模型在长视频中发现并验证关键时间片段，配合自动构建的TimeThink-RFT-20K数据集，在多项视频推理与时序定位任务上取得SOTA的开源视频RL表现。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 1) 将推理分解为一系列“时间线索步骤”，每步指向候选时间区间并陈述相应推理；2) 设计步级时间过程奖励，对每个被引用区间的正确性/相关性进行局部归因；3) 构建联合优化目标：过程(过程奖励) + 结果(最终答案正确性)的权衡；4) 构建TimeThink-RFT-20K数据集，以自动化方式从视频与标注中派生出时序证据片段以支撑可扩展训练。

Conclusion: 显式建模“时间线索步骤”并采用步级过程奖励与结果奖励的联合优化，能够有效引导Video-LLM在长视频中发现并利用关键证据，提升可解释性与性能；TimeThink与其自动化数据集为可扩展的视频推理RL训练提供了有效途径。

Abstract: Video reasoning requires models to identify and verify temporally localized evidence within long video sequences. Recent Video Large Language Models (Video-LLMs) have shown promising reasoning abilities when aligned with reinforcement learning, yet existing approaches typically rely on outcome-based rewards that supervise only the final prediction. Such supervision provides limited guidance on how models should discover the relevant temporal evidence during intermediate reasoning. In this work, we propose TimeThink, a reinforcement learning framework that explicitly guides temporal evidence discovery in Video-LLMs. Our key idea is to treat temporal clue steps as the fundamental optimization primitive of video reasoning, where each reasoning step references a candidate time interval in the video. We introduce a step-wise temporal process reward that provides localized credit assignment for these clues and a joint process--outcome optimization objective that balances reasoning fidelity with task correctness. To enable scalable training, we construct TimeThink-RFT-20K, a dataset with automatically derived temporal evidence segments. Extensive experiments across video reasoning, temporal grounding, and general video understanding benchmarks show that TimeThink consistently improves both temporal localization and reasoning performance, achieving state-of-the-art results among open-source video RL models.

This work explores modeling spinal degeneration as a continuous severity ranking problem. We introduce SpineRankNet, a framework that learns scalar severity scores from lumbar spinal MRI, and compare it against multi-class classification and ordinal regression. Using multiple degeneration measures from the Genodisc dataset, we show that a model trained using a ranking loss to produce a continuous score enables fine-grained ordering of MRI scans. Furthermore, the ordinal grading classes can be recovered from the score with comparable accuracy to those from a model trained directly for classification. ### [291] [Green for Go, Red for No: Visual Grounding via Semantic Segmentation for VLA Navigation Policies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05122)
*Adrian Szvoren,Dimitrios Kanoulas,Nilufer Tuptuk*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: VLA在自然语言与视觉目标驱动的机器人导航中易受感知干扰与场景歧义影响，导致路径偏差与错误决策。作者希望检验并量化“视觉落地（visual grounding）”是否能缓解这些问题。

Method: 提出基于SegFormer的实时语义分割，将可通行区域渲染为绿色、不可通行为红色，作为输入增强。评估两种设置：仅在观察上分割（observation-only）与同时在观察和目标上增强（observation-goal）。使用OmniVLA在Grand Tour数据集上，比较不同指令长度与目标类型（文本指令 vs. 图像目标）下的性能。

Abstract: Vision-language-action (VLA) models enable robot navigation from natural language and visual goals, but remain susceptible to perceptual distractions and ambiguous scene interpretations. This paper presents the first empirical evaluation of visual grounding for VLA navigation policies. We propose a real-time segmentation-based grounding method that highlights traversable areas in green and non-traversable areas in red using SegFormer. Two variants are evaluated: observation-only segmentation and joint observation-goal augmentation. Using OmniVLA on the Grand Tour dataset, we show that visual grounding reduces the mean waypoint error by 27-44% at the farthest waypoint, depending on the instruction length. The benefits are greater for long instructions than for short instructions, and grounding provides little improvement for image goals. Normalized error analysis indicates that grounding primarily acts as a trajectory length regularizer, reducing the predicted path length by 30% without improving per-unit-distance reasoning. Our results indicate that visual grounding offers a simple, computationally inexpensive method to improve VLA navigation without model retraining, although it cannot compensate for missing training signals in out-of-distribution instructions.

### [292] [UNIVERSE: Unified Video Action Models for Autonomous Driving with Flexible Mask-Modulated Modality Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05133)

TL;DR: UNIVERSE 提出将视频预测与轨迹生成统一到单一掩码调制的Diffusion Transformer中，通过共享参数与密集视频监督，显著提升自动驾驶动作的跨域泛化，并在保持精度的同时以可见性掩码实现无泄漏、可高效的仅轨迹推理（4.3×提速）。在NAVSIM达91.0 PDMS，优于双DiT基线，且零样本迁移到nuScenes与Bench2Drive表现强劲。

Conclusion: 统一的视频-动作扩散Transformer让视频密集监督直接作用于轨迹去噪，显著提升跨域泛化与部署效率；模态解耦掩码确保因果性与灵活推理模式。UNIVERSE在标准基准与零样本迁移上优于分离式架构，验证了单模型统一与掩码解耦的有效性。

Abstract: World Action Models (WAMs) have shown strong potential for improving action generalization in autonomous driving by using future video prediction as dense supervision for scene dynamics and temporal causality. However, it remains unclear which architecture better transfers video-modeling benefits to trajectory generation. Existing cascaded or dual-DiT designs separate video imagination from action prediction, weakening the transfer of video-learned world dynamics to the trajectory branch: the action model may still overfit dataset-specific driving priors, while the video model only indirectly regularizes planning. We propose UNIVERSE, a unified video-action model built upon a single mask-modulated Diffusion Transformer. By co-training future video latents and ego-trajectory tokens within shared generative parameters, UNIVERSE allows dense video supervision to directly shape trajectory denoising, leading to stronger cross-domain action generalization. To ensure causal validity and efficient deployment, we introduce a Modality-Decoupling Visibility Mask, which shares historical context across modalities while blocking mutual attention between future video and trajectory tokens. This prevents future-target leakage and enables trajectory-only inference by removing future-video denoising at test time, achieving a $4.3\times$ speedup over joint video-action rollout while maintaining comparable planning accuracy. The same model also supports video-only and joint video-action rollouts. Experiments show that UNIVERSE achieves 91.0 PDMS on NAVSIM (vs. 89.6 for the Two-DiT variant), and demonstrates strong zero-shot transfer to nuScenes and Bench2Drive without fine-tuning, while ablations confirm the importance of single-DiT unification, video co-training, and mask-based modality decoupling.

### [293] [Fully Rotation-Equivariant Spectral-Spatial Learning for Multispectral Object Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05148)
*Peng Zhang,Tingfa Xu,Shuaihao Han,Jianan Li*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出FressDet：一种端到端、全旋转等变的多光谱目标检测框架，连续建模光谱并在金字塔尺度上自适应融合光谱-空间信息，参数更少、性能SOTA。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有多光谱检测器存在三大痛点：1) 光谱处理离散、无法体现光谱的连续有序性；2) 在特征金字塔不同尺度上，光谱/空间线索可靠性随尺度变化且缺乏稳定融合机制；3) 缺少对任意方向目标的显式旋转等变几何先验，导致旋转扰动下表现不稳。

Method: 提出FressDet，由三部分组成：1) SpeIW：基于坐标条件的隐式场进行查询式光谱重采样，实现单调、保序的光谱“隐式形变”，刻画连续有序的光谱结构；2) ReCoW：旋转等变一致性加权，根据分支（光谱/空间）在各金字塔层的置信与一致性自适应加权融合，强化信息、抑制噪声；3) Oriented-aware head：利用群索引特征（旋转群）在不复制参数的情况下稳定预测任意朝向的目标。整体实现跨尺度、对旋转鲁棒的光谱-空间联合表征学习。

Result: 在三个公开基准上达到SOTA，同时参数量减少约93%，在任意平面旋转扰动下仍保持鲁棒检测性能。

Conclusion: FressDet通过隐式连续光谱建模、自适应旋转等变融合与面向方向的检测头，构建了高判别、强鲁棒的光谱-空间表征，实现轻量且泛化性强的多光谱目标检测。

Abstract: Existing multispectral detectors are limited by discrete spectral processing, a scale-dependent shift in the relative reliability of spectral and spatial cues across pyramid levels, and the lack of explicit rotation-equivariant geometric priors for arbitrarily oriented objects. To tackle these limitations, we propose FressDet, a fully rotation-equivariant spectral-spatial learning framework for multispectral object detection, capable of capturing the continuous, ordered nature of spectral structure and enabling reliable spectral-spatial fusion across pyramid levels under arbitrary in-plane rotations. FressDet integrates three complementary components. Spectral Implicit Warp (SpeIW) enables query-based spectral resampling via a coordinate-conditioned implicit field, yielding a monotone, order-preserving warp. Rotation-Equivariant Consistency Weighting (ReCoW) adaptively fuses spectral and spatial branches based on branch reliability, reinforcing informative cues while suppressing noise across pyramid levels. The oriented-aware head exploits group-indexed features to stably predict oriented objects without parameter replication. Taken together, FressDet learns more discriminative and robust spectral-spatial representations even under rotational perturbations. By achieving state-of-the-art performance with 93% fewer parameters on three public benchmarks, FressDet demonstrates its effectiveness and generalizability.

### [294] [Claim-Level Rubric Rewards for Video Caption Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05150)
*Mingqi Gao,Hongyuan Dong,Yifei Chen,Zhisheng Zhong,Zheng Ruan,Wenjin Hou,Yu Chen,Han Hu,Yansong Tang*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有强化学习中文本生成的奖励要么整体打分（易被文风欺骗、难保事实性），要么与参考对齐（僵硬、限制开放生成的完整性与多样性）。需要一种既保事实又不束缚表达的奖励方式。

Method: 将视频描述分解为带类别意识的原子主张，通过结构化评分量表（rubric）逐条核验，把整体评价转化为更易可靠的主张级验证，从而形成奖励信号（Claim-Level Rubric Rewards, CuRe）。

Result: CuRe把复杂的整体评估分解为可验证的细粒度单元，降低奖励黑客风险并增强事实一致性与多样性保持；在稠密视频描述的强化学习场景中更稳健。

Conclusion: 主张级、结构化的奖励建模能克服整体式与参考式奖励的固有限制，为开放式多样生成任务提供更准确、可扩展的奖励设计路径。

Abstract: In this paper, we introduce Claim-Level Rubric Rewards (CuRe), a structured reward framework designed to address the reward-design bottleneck in reinforcement learning for dense video captioning. Existing reward designs generally fall into two categories: holistic response-level judgment across heterogeneous criteria, or alignment-based evaluation against reference captions. However, both paradigms suffer from fundamental limitations. Holistic rewards struggle to ensure factual accuracy and are prone to stylistic reward hacking, while reference-based rewards overly rely on rigid textual alignment, failing to preserve the completeness and diversity inherent to open-ended generation tasks. To address these challenges, CuRe reformulates reward modeling as fine-grained claim-level verification. Specifically, CuRe decomposes captions into category-aware atomic claims through a structured rubric, converting holistic evaluation into simpler and more reliable claim-level verification.

### [295] [FSDC-DETR: A Frequency-Spatial Domain Collaborative DETR for Small Object Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05176)
*Aiwen Liu,Chengguang Zhu,Gang Wang,Dandan Zhu,Haodong Lin,Yan Wang,Huiyu Zhou,Zhiyi Pan*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出FSDC-DETR，以显式结合频域与空间域信息，面向小目标检测，显著提升高频细节保留与跨尺度传播，在VisDrone与AITODv2上取得SOTA与明显AP提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有检测器在小目标检测中易受隐式频率混叠与截断影响，空间聚合过程与频域退化相互纠缠，导致高频细节（对小目标至关重要）无法有效保留与传递。需要一种能显式建模并协同利用空间与频域表示的框架，以缓解频率退化并强化跨尺度传播。

Method: 提出FSDC-DETR的协同频-空Transformer框架：1) DBFSAF双分支频-空自适应融合，增强频率多样性并自适应获取判别性的频-空表示；2) 混合编码器中设计频-空交互机制，逐步将信息向解码器传播；3) SFS-FF实现“分流式”频-空特征聚合，构建双向交互与逐级跨尺度传播；4) FSD-Down在尺度变换中动态下采样，尽可能保留高频响应，减少多尺度融合过程的频率退化。

Result: 在VisDrone-DET2019与AITODv2上达到SOTA：整体AP分别提升6.4和6.6；小目标AP提升6.8和6.9，显示在SOD场景的显著优势。

Conclusion: 显式的频-空协同建模与动态下采样可有效缓解频率混叠与退化，增强高频信息保真度与跨尺度传播，从而显著提升小目标检测性能；FSDC-DETR验证了该设计的有效性并取得SOTA。

Abstract: Small object detection (SOD) remains a challenging task in real-world applications. Despite recent advances, existing detectors remain limited by rigid processing that entangle spatial aggregation with implicit frequency aliasing and truncation, leading to inadequate preservation of high-frequency components for SOD. To tackle these limitations, we propose a Frequency-Spatial Domain Collaborative Detection Transformer (FSDC-DETR), a novel collaborative framework that explicitly models complementary spatial and frequency representations. Specifically, we first introduce Dual-Branch Frequency-Spatial Adaptive Fusion (DBFSAF) to enhance frequency diversity and adaptively capture frequency-spatial domain discriminative representations. Building on these representations, a frequency-spatial interaction scheme is further explored within the hybrid encoder to enable progressive feature propagation to the decoder. In particular, structure-aware frequency-spatial aggregation is achieved through Shunt Frequency-Spatial Feature Fusion (SFS-FF), establishing bidirectional interaction and progressive cross-scale propagation between frequency and spatial representations for coherent discriminative modeling. Meanwhile, informative high-frequency responses are preserved during scale transitions through Frequency-Spatial Dynamic Downsampling (FSD-Down), thereby minimizing frequency degradation throughout multi-scale fusion for the precise SOD. Experimental results demonstrate that FSDC-DETR achieves state-of-the-art performance, improving AP by 6.4 on VisDrone-DET2019 and 6.6 on AITODv2, with gains of 6.8 and 6.9 AP for small objects. The code is available at github.com/nevereverinsomnia/FSDC-DETR.

The retinal-image fold constructs an interpretable $X1234$ phenotype from vessel maps, lesion evidence, image embeddings, and AutoMorph biomarkers through spatial $X_{12}$ and Jacobian $X_{34}$ branches. The NHANES fold models systemic exposures, covariates, a same-subject retinal mediator family $R^*$, and downstream outcome families. $X1234$ is used for retinal support and pathway prioritisation, while $R^*$ is used for participant-level pathway summaries.   <summary>Details</summary>

Owing to its feed-forward and training-free architecture, the neural model requires only a small number of interpretable parameters and is well suited for real-time embedded implementation. Event cameras provide low-latency, low-power, and high-dynamic-range visual sensing by asynchronously transmitting brightness-change events. However, their performance can be degraded by event noise, including temporal noise and junction-leakage-induced activity, particularly under low-light conditions. Moreover, effective integration between event-based visual representations and biologically inspired neural processing remains under-explored. To address these challenges, we propose an event-driven computational framework that combines time-surface encoding for front-end event representation with a fly optic-lobe-inspired neural network for foreground motion-direction estimation. Abstract: Self-supervised learning (SSL) is designed to learn generic, transferable representations rather than representations optimized for a single task. Most geospatial benchmarks evaluate representations solely through downstream tasks, providing limited insight into the information encoded within the representation itself. We ask a different question: do SSL representations of satellite imagery preserve statistical associations with environmental variables that co-vary with the imaging process? ### [299] [A Multimodal Reasoning Typology for Grounding Chart-Image Coherence in Science Communication](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05222)
*Avina Nakarmi,Sohom Sen,Xun Song,Sreyashi Samaddar,Aritra Dasgupta*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 论文提出一个关于图表、图像与字幕共同构成“多模态单元”的推理难度分级（R1–R5），用以衡量读者从三者中推断科学主张所需的解释工作量，并用专家与非专家评审VLM描述的实验验证该分级能预测一致与分歧之处。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于传播中的奠基理论，作者与一名神经科学专家自下而上分析79篇TBI论文与32个图表-图像配对，归纳出R1–R5推理缺口类型学，刻画图、像、文如何共同构建主张（如重复数据、量化局部结构、将图像投影到外部变量、审计图像性主张、或共同建构单独无法成立的框架）。随后进行一项用户研究：1名领域专家与3名非专家对25对配图的VLM描述做判断，观察不同级别上的一致性与分歧。

Result: 分级能系统性预测专家与非专家对VLM描述判断的一致或分歧点，定位那些主要由情境知识而非图形本身维系连贯性的环节；从而为识别“奠基”成功或断裂提供可操作机制。

Abstract: Charts and images appear together throughout scientific publications, yet most computational work does not characterize their coherence. We argue that a chart, its accompanying image, and the caption that links them form a multimodal unit, and that the inferential work required to read it varies systematically. To capture this variation, we develop a typology of reasoning gaps, R1 through R5, that characterizes how chart, image, and text jointly convey a scientific claim, and the interpretive work this demands of the reader. Some pairs restate the same data, while in other pairs, charts are used to quantify a structure the image localizes, project image content onto an external variable, audit an image-based claim, or jointly construct a frame that neither panel can establish alone. The typology is anchored in the grounding theory of communication and was derived bottom-up, with a neuroscience expert, from a corpus of 79 traumatic brain injury papers and 32 chart-image pairs. Crucially, the levels provide a systematic mechanism for identifying where grounding succeeds or breaks down, rather than leaving it to subjective inference. We show this in a study in which a domain expert and three non-experts judge vision-language model (VLM) descriptions of 25 pairs: the level predicts where their judgments align and where they diverge, isolating the points at which contextual knowledge, not the figure, carries coherence. This typology thus offers figure designers a systematic way to balance text against chart-image pairs, bridging the expert-to-non-expert divide in reading a scientific takeaway.

  <summary>Details</summary>

To fill this gap, we present GUSH3R (Gaussian-Unified Scene Human 3D Reconstruction), a feed-forward framework for online dynamic human-scene reconstruction. From a monocular human-scene video, our method reconstructs dynamic humans (everyone) and static scenes (everywhere) in a single forward pass (all at once) as 3D Gaussian Splatting (3DGS) primitives (as gaussians), which are geometrically consistent and capable of novel view synthesis. *Zelin Fu,Bin Tan,Changjiang Sun,Shaohui Liu,Kecheng Zheng,Yinghao Xu,Xing Zhu,Yujun Shen,Nan Xue*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出一种以边界为中心的自监督预训练：通过学习亚像素级边界表示并用边界承载token作掩码目标，提升密集视觉表征；在DINOv3强基线上扩展成LingBot‑Vision，显著提升多任务表现，尤其推动深度补全从LingBot‑Depth 1.0到2.0。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有视觉基础模型强调语义不变性，牺牲了精细空间理解；而几何感知离不开边界和形状不连续等线索，因此需要一种能强化密集空间结构表征的预训练原则。

Method: 提出Masked Boundary Modeling（MBM）：先自监督学习亚像素边界表示；再将含边界信息的token作为掩码学习目标，驱动密集视觉token学习。将该框架规模化，构建LingBot‑Vision，并以DINOv3作为对比/基线。

Result: 在多种下游密集视觉任务上取得优于DINOv3的效果；在深度任务上显著提升，促成LingBot‑Depth从1.0升级到2.0，提升深度估计/补全质量。

Conclusion: 边界建模并非仅限于线段检测，而是可扩展的预训练范式，能学习到结构化、度量化、可行动的空间视觉表征，对具身智能关键的深度感知尤为有效。

Abstract: Dense spatial perception is essential for physical intelligence, where visual systems are expected to recover structured, metric, and actionable representations from pixel observations. Modern visual foundation models tend to prioritize semantic invariance, often at the expense of detailed spatial understanding. In this work, we study vision pretraining through a boundary-centric lens, motivated by the premise that boundaries and shape discontinuities offer essential cues for perceiving geometric properties. Concretely, we propose masked boundary modeling, a self-supervised paradigm that dynamically learns sub-pixel boundary representations and subsequently leverages the discovered boundary-bearing tokens as masked targets to facilitate dense visual token learning. By scaling this framework, we develop LingBot-Vision and demonstrate its efficacy across a diverse set of downstream vision tasks with DINOv3 as a strong baseline. Remarkably, LingBot-Vision drives the progression from LingBot-Depth 1.0 to LingBot-Depth 2.0 for depth completion, and thereby yields enhanced depth estimation, a key pillar for embodied artificial intelligence. Our findings reveal that boundary modeling goes beyond simple line segments and instead serves as a scalable pretraining principle for learning spatially structured visual representations.

</details>


### [302] [Repurposing CLIP to Localize at Pixel Level](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05253)
*Jiaxiang Fang,Shiqiang Ma,Jing Wang,Siyu Chen,Fei Guo,Shengfeng He*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出CLIPix，将CLIP从图像级开放集定位扩展到像素级分割：回溯分类以提取对象注意区域为初始线索，结合抗噪校正与定位嵌入，实现高分辨率、任意类别的精确分割，并在PASCAL与COCO上达SOTA。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有CLIP在开放集图像级定位表现强，但直接用于像素级密集预测受全局特征偏置影响，导致噪声与边界不精确；需要一种方法在不牺牲泛化能力的前提下，把图像级语义对齐迁移到精细分割。

Method: 1) 回溯CLIP分类过程，提取类别相关的注意/激活区域作为像素级初始定位线索；2) 噪声抵抗校正（Noise-Resistant Correction）抑制由全局偏置带来的噪声并细化线索；3) 定位嵌入（Localization Embedding）融合定位与细节特征，支持高分辨率分割；整体以CLIP为骨干，保持其开放集泛化。

Result: 在PASCAL与COCO数据集上进行大量实验，相比现有方法取得最新最优（SOTA）性能，显示出更高的定位精度与分割质量。

Conclusion: CLIPix能将CLIP的开放集能力有效下放到像素级，实现对任意对象的高精度分割；抗噪校正与定位嵌入是关键，且保持了跨类别的良好泛化。

Abstract: Large-scale Vision-Language Models like CLIP have demonstrated impressive open-set localization capabilities at the image level. However, adapting this capability to pixel-level dense prediction poses challenges due to global feature biases. In this paper, we introduce CLIPix, a simple yet effective framework that repurposes CLIP to perform pixel-level localization. By tracing back CLIP's classification process, CLIPix identifies object-specific attentive regions and repurposes them as pixel-level localization cues. To address noise introduced by global biases, we propose a Noise-Resistant Correction strategy, refining these cues for more precise segmentation. Additionally, we introduce a Localization Embedding strategy to integrate both localization and enriched detail information, enabling accurate, high-resolution segmentation. Our approach preserves CLIP's generalization strength and unlocks its potential for segmenting arbitrary objects. Extensive experiments on the PASCAL and COCO datasets demonstrate that CLIPix achieves state-of-the-art performance, underscoring its effectiveness.

### [303] [Shifting from Discrete to Continuous Reference Data: QSM-Derived Horizontal Tree Biomass Distribution for Deep Learning Biomass Estimation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05260)
*Nils Griese,Christoph Kleinn,Nils Nölke*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 论文提出用连续的水平生物量分布（HBD）作为激光雷达地上生物量（AGB）估计的参考，替代传统离散样地汇总，显著减小小样地的边界效应并提升模型性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 基于LiDAR的AGB估计常使用样地级汇总指标，但在小样地中易受边界效应影响，导致不确定性增大与精度下降。作者希望通过避免样地边界截断误差，改进小尺度训练与预测的可靠性。

Method: 从定量结构模型（QSM）连续映射出HBD参考，构建并训练稀疏3D U-Net，对比三种AGB参考：传统森林清查（FI）样地汇总、无边界效应的QSM样地汇总、以及连续HBD。训练样地面积从100到2500 m^2进行扩展与评估。

Result: 在小样地条件下，基于QSM的模型系统性优于FI基线。以100 m^2为例，HBD参考相对均方根误差（RRMSE）降低16.84±4.37%，R^2提升0.22±0.05。

Conclusion: 以HBD替代样地级汇总能校正边界效应，特别在小样地中显著提升AGB估计模型表现；建议在小尺度训练与应用中采用连续HBD作为参考。

Abstract: Conventional modeling approaches for LiDAR-based above-ground biomass (AGB) estimation rely on discrete plot-level inventory aggregates. This methodology introduces boundary-effect uncertainties that may severely degrade model performance within small field plots. To solve this limitation, we evaluate a Horizontal Biomass Distribution (HBD) reference mapped continuously from Quantitative Structure Models (QSMs). We trained a sparse 3D U-Net on simulated broadleaved forest structures using three AGB reference types: a standard forest inventory (FI) plot-level aggregate, an edge-effect-free QSM plot-level aggregate, and a continuous HBD mapping. Evaluating training plot sizes scaling from 100 to 2500 $m^2$ , QSM-based models systematically outperformed FI approaches at small plot sizes. Specifically, for 100 $m^2$ plots, the HBD reference reduced the relative root mean square error (RRMSE) by 16.84 $\pm$ 4.37 % and increased $R^2$ by 0.22 $\pm$ 0.05 against the FI baseline. By replacing plot level aggregates with HBDs as AGB reference, this methodology corrects for edge-effects and shows that using an HBD-based reference enhances model performance for small plot sizes.

### [304] [FlowMark: Mask-Guided Video Watermarking](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05261)
*Vishal Asnani,Shruti Agarwal,John Collomosse*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: FlowMark是一种由自动预测目标掩膜引导的视频水印框架，端到端训练，通过内容自适应掩膜与噪声增强实现对压缩、几何与时序编辑的鲁棒，同时保持高感知质量，可在真实社媒重编码下可靠提取128位水印。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有区域水印需要人工提供掩膜，难以规模化且易产生视觉闪烁，对视频原生时序编辑和社媒重编码的鲁棒性不足。需要一种自动选择嵌入区域、与视频动态一致、在多种扰动下稳定的水印方法。

Method: 提出FlowMark：1) 训练Mask Predictor自动预测适合嵌入的对象/区域；2) 区域感知编码器在选区内嵌入水印；3) 采用噪声与多种失真（压缩、几何变换、时序操作）增强进行端到端联合训练；4) 内容自适应的时空一致掩膜使水印随运动保持相干，减少闪烁；5) 解码器在各种失真后恢复128位信息。

Result: 在图像与视频数据集上，能以最高约50.08 dB PSNR嵌入并可靠恢复128位消息；对压缩、几何变换、帧交换/插入/删除/重采样/插值等时序编辑以及YouTube、Facebook等重编码均具鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 自动掩膜引导与区域感知编码结合的FlowMark在保持高视觉质量的同时，显著提升对视频原生时序编辑和社媒管线的鲁棒性，为内容溯源、时间真实性验证和视频完整性保护提供了有效方案。

Abstract: We present FlowMark, a video watermarking framework guided by automatically predicted object masks. In contrast to prior region-based approaches that require user-supplied mask guidance, FlowMark learns to identify optimal regions for watermark embedding through a dedicated Mask Predictor network. Our end-to-end trainable architecture combines region-aware encoding with noise-augmented training to ensure robustness against compression, geometric transformations, and content variation, while preserving high perceptual quality. Our content-adaptive masking keeps watermark signals coherent with natural video dynamics, effectively eliminating perceptual flicker. Beyond compression robustness, FlowMark maintains reliable watermark recovery under video-native temporal edits (e.g., frame swap, insertion, deletion, resampling, and interpolation) and real-world social media distribution pipelines (e.g., YouTube and Facebook re-encoding). Experimental results on both image and video datasets show that FlowMark reliably embeds $128$-bit messages with up to $50.08$ dB PSNR, offering strong performance for content provenance, temporal authenticity verification, and video integrity protection.

### [305] [Learning Probabilistic Embeddings for Unsupervised Action Segmentation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05263)
*Shuai Li,Duc Manh Vu,Juergen Gall*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出在无监督长视频动作分割中，用高斯分布的概率嵌入替代传统确定性嵌入，并结合最优传输(OT)生成伪标签；在多数据集上达到或超过SOTA，MoF最高+20.7%、F1最高+19.0%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法在联合表示学习与聚类框架下，利用OT交替生成伪标签并优化参数，但因帧表示是确定性嵌入，迭代易陷入局部最优，限制了无监督动作分割性能。需要一种能更好探索解空间、缓解伪标签与表示相互依赖导致的收敛僵化的方法。

Method: 将帧级表示建模为高斯分布的概率嵌入；在每轮OT估计伪标签前从分布中采样，以引入不确定性与探索；训练过程仍采用交替优化：采样—用OT生成伪标签—基于伪标签更新表示网络参数；最终用OT做时序分割。

Result: 在多款具有挑战性的时序动作分割数据集上，性能与SOTA相当或更优；相较确定性嵌入基线，MoF提升最高20.7%，F1提升最高19.0%；代码已开源。

Conclusion: 概率化帧表示与OT结合能缓解局部最优与伪标签反馈回路问题，提升无监督时序动作分割效果；为该任务提供一种稳健且易集成的替代于确定性嵌入的框架。

Abstract: This paper concerns the problem of unsupervised temporal action segmentation for long, untrimmed videos. Recent successful approaches follow a joint representation learning and clustering paradigm, where optimal transport (OT) is adopted to produce pseudo labels for learning frame representations. These approaches alternate between estimating pseudo labels using OT and optimizing the parameters with gradient descent during training, where OT is used for obtaining the final temporal action segmentation. A major limitation of these works is that they learn a deterministic embedding for frame representations. The iterative procedure between learning deterministic embeddings based on pseudo labels and estimating pseudo labels from the learned embedding can thus get quickly stuck in a local optimum. As an alternative, we thus propose to learn a probabilistic embedding for frame representations. The embeddings are modeled by Gaussian distributions and we sample from the distributions before estimating the pseudo labels. We evaluate our approach on several challenging temporal action segmentation datasets and achieve results comparable to, and in some cases, better than the state of the art. Compared to baselines with deterministic embeddings, our approach improves MoF up to 20.7\% and F1-score up to 19.0\%. Our code is available at https://github.com/derkbreeze/PEOT.

### [306] [SteelBench: Evaluating Vision-Language Models in Real-World Industrial Environments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05264)
*Suryanarayana Reddy Yarrabothula,Manisha Chawla,Kunal Sinha,Gagan Raj Gupta,Sashank Lekkala,Ashirvadhan Dosapati,Saikamal Nannuri,Katragadda Ajay RamaSwamy Chowdary Gowtham*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: STEELBENCH 是面向工业监控（CCTV）的多任务诊断基准，用于评测VLM在工厂真实环境中对“每名工人动作识别+安全规则推理+标注溯源”的能力；结果显示未经审计的模型生成标注会显著抬高同家族模型分数（最高+17pp），最佳模型动作准确率仅42.6%（人类84.6%），且在稳健性、校准与安全判断上分裂，无模型通过超过2/5的诊断。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有视频基准多来自日常/第一视角/模拟工业场景，缺乏真实工业CCTV的极端观测条件（远距离、粉尘蒸汽、低照、眩光、遮挡、多活动重叠），也未系统考察VLM在安全规则推理与标注来源偏差（provenance）的影响。

Method: 构建STEELBENCH：从149小时厂区实拍与10,024候选片段中，使用时间去重、类别均衡、按可见度分层抽样，筛得1,345条密集标注片段；对每名工人给出动作、PPE属性、空间语境与安全规则标签。提出“溯源审计协议”，量化模型辅助标注对评测的影响与对真值来源敏感性，并提供经专家复核的人类参考。对来自4种架构家族的9个VLM进行多维评测（识别、稳健性、校准、安全推理与诊断检查）。

Result: 未经审计的VLM生成真值会使同家族模型准确率虚高，最高+17个百分点。最佳VLM动作准确率仅42.6%，显著落后于人类84.6%。即便动作预测正确，仍有37–58%的样例给出错误安全判断；在5项诊断检查中，无模型通过超过2项，表现呈碎片化。

Conclusion: 真实工业监控环境对VLM提出更高挑战：动作识别、稳健性、校准与安全推理均显著不足；评测应纳入标注溯源审计以避免被模型生成标注“自我强化”所误导。STEELBENCH提供公开数据与协议，为面向安全关键工业场景的模型发展与公平评测奠定基线。

Abstract: Existing video benchmarks evaluate action recognition on consumer videos, egocentric recordings, or simulated industrial environments. They do not test vision-language models under the visual and procedural conditions of real industrial CCTV, where workers appear as distant figures amid dust, steam, low light, glare, occlusion, and overlapping activities. We introduce STEELBENCH, a diagnostic benchmark for industrial surveillance that jointly evaluates per-worker activity recognition, safety-rule reasoning, and annotation provenance. SteelBench contains 1,345 densely annotated clips, curated from 149 hours of operational plant footage and 10,024 candidate clips using temporal deduplication, class balancing, and visibility-aware stratified sampling. Each clip includes dense per-worker action labels, PPE attributes, spatial context, and safety-rule annotations. Because model-assisted annotation can shape the labels later used for model evaluation, SteelBench includes a provenance-aware audit protocol. The protocol measures label influence, evaluates sensitivity to ground-truth provenance, and reports a human reference from expert-reviewed labels. Applying this audit, we find that unaudited VLM-sourced ground truth can inflate same-family model accuracy by up to 17 percentage points. Across nine VLMs from four architectural families, the best model reaches only 42.6% action accuracy, compared with an 84.6% human benchmark. Performance also fragments across recognition, robustness, calibration, and safety reasoning. Even when models predict the correct action, 37-58% of cases still yield incorrect safety judgments, and no model passes more than 2 of 5 diagnostic checks. The dataset is publicly available on Hugging Face.

### [307] [Is the Geometry Doing the Work? An Operating-Point Audit of Hierarchy in Hyperbolic Vision-Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05268)
*Jaeyoung Kim,Eunseok Kim,Dongsuk Jang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 论文审计三类超曲率视觉-语言模型，发现曲率资源未被真正使用、圆锥/径向机制失效、层级评测被角度或监督混淆；提出机制解释与五数字几何报告以校准未来层级化主张。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 社区近年用双曲几何来建模层级与蕴含，但“是否真的在用几何”常以曲率参数拍脑袋判断，缺少可操作的诊断；同时不少工作报告了层级/检索收益，却可能由非几何因素驱动。作者欲给出必要条件审计，澄清哪些机制在工作、哪些是表象。

Method: 提出一组必要条件诊断：基于无量纲运行点 √c·ρ、H(u) 近欧度量；对径向深度、蕴含圆锥与遍历（traversal）的可操作性做受控读出与敏感度分析；在固定 GRIT 快照上对 MERU、HyCoCLIP、PHyCLIP 多检查点与受控干预（如释放曲率下界）进行审计；分离角向距离、盒/组合监督等因素对“层级外观”指标的贡献；给出机制性解释与一个“孔径恒等式”（当 √c·ρ≤2K 时圆锥饱和）。

Result: 发现三类失效：1) 曲率不活跃：运行点近欧(H≈1)，无收敛检查点达 √c·ρ>1；放开曲率下界只改变曲率与范数，不动运行点且下游性能无显著损失。2) 圆锥与遍历机制不可用：圆锥不工作/饱和/失配，分级遍历在受控读出下失败；定向径向深度仅略高于乱序基线，唯一残存的“原生关系”也不工作。3) 层级化评测欠定：类目相关性由角距离承担，粗粒度检索提升随盒/组合监督而非曲率变化。

Conclusion: 现有发布配方并未实现其几何动机的径向/圆锥机制；所谓层级收益多由非曲率因素驱动。作者给出机制解释：蕴含目标允许低曲率-宽圆锥捷径，且参数无关的孔径恒等式定位了训练收敛的“饱和边界”；真正关闭蕴含后不再受该边界束缚。提出“五数字几何报告”作为今后层级主张的最低审计标准。

Abstract: Whether a hyperbolic representation model uses its geometry cannot be read off its curvature parameter: what matters is the dimensionless operating point $\sqrt{c}ρ$ and whether the radial and cone machinery is active there. We develop a battery of necessary-condition diagnostics and audit three published hyperbolic vision-language families -- MERU, HyCoCLIP, and PHyCLIP -- across released checkpoints and controlled interventions on a fixed GRIT snapshot, identifying three failure modes. First, curvature is not an active resource: the operating point stays near-Euclidean ($H(u)\approx 1$; no audited converged checkpoint reaches $\sqrt{c}ρ>1$), and releasing the curvature floor moves curvature and norms but keeps the operating point near-Euclidean, without substantial downstream degradation. Second, the cone and traversal machinery is measured inoperative: entailment cones are inactive, saturated, or misaligned, and graded traversal fails under controlled readouts, while directed radial depth is a bounded non-detection above shuffle-null controls at quantified sensitivity; the one surviving native-relation residual remains non-operative. Third, hierarchy-looking evaluations are underdetermined: taxonomy correlations are carried by angular distance, and coarse-retrieval gains track box/compositional supervision, not curvature. A mechanistic account explains why: the entailment objective admits a low-curvature, wide-cone shortcut, and a parameter-free aperture identity (cones saturate iff $\sqrt{c}ρ\le 2K$) locates the edge where every entailment-trained unclamped run settles; entailment-off runs show no arrest there. The shortcut is the dominant accelerator of collapse, not its sole cause. These formulations, as released, do not instantiate the radial/cone mechanism their geometry motivates; we distill the audit into a five-number geometry report for future hierarchy claims.

</details>


### [308] [Erasing Without Collateral Damage: Precise Concept Removal in Diffusion Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05274)
*Parth Upman,Nishita Jain,Shreyank N Gowda*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: CARE提出一种无需训练的精确概念擦除算子，在保持非目标概念的同时有效移除目标概念，对扩散模型跨注意力值空间进行闭式编辑。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有无训练擦除方法在值空间沿目标概念方向做投影/去除，混淆了“目标身份信号”和与非目标共享的视觉结构，导致对相关概念的附带破坏；需要一种既能有效擦除、又尽量保留非目标概念的机制。

Method: 提出CARE（Kept-subspace-Aware Erasure）：用一组被保留的概念锚点构建“保留子空间”，据此从原始目标方向中分离出与保留子空间正交的、感知保留子空间的擦除方向；在跨注意力的value空间以闭式算子进行编辑，无需微调；通过单一收缩参数控制擦除-保留权衡；投影形式可保证保留子空间不被改变，并给出最小扰动解释。

Result: 在标准概念擦除协议下，针对实例、风格与名人等目标，能在保持与目标相关但非目标的概念上显著减少破坏，同时实现与现有方法相当或更好的擦除强度；仅需可忽略的离线计算开销。

Conclusion: CARE通过保留子空间感知的方向构造，在不训练的前提下实现更精细的概念擦除与更好的非目标保真，提供可控的擦除-保留权衡与理论上的最小扰动/不变性保证。

Abstract: Training-free concept erasure is an attractive mechanism for controlling text-to-image diffusion models, but precise erasure often comes at the cost of damaging semantically related non-target concepts. Existing value-space methods remove the component of each cross-attention value along the target concept direction, implicitly treating target identity and shared visual structure as the same signal. We argue that this is the source of much of the collateral damage in prior preservation. We introduce CARE, a closed-form concept erasure operator that replaces the raw target direction with a kept-subspace-aware direction computed from a small bank of retained concept anchors. The resulting edit is applied directly in cross-attention value space, requires no model fine-tuning, and adds only a negligible offline computation. A single shrinkage parameter controls the erase-preserve trade-off. We further show that the operator admits a minimum-disturbance interpretation and, in its projection form, leaves the kept subspace invariant. Experiments under the standard concept-erasure protocol show that our method preserves non-target concepts more faithfully while maintaining competitive erasure across instance, style, and celebrity concepts. Code: https://github.com/parthupman/care

</details>


### [309] [ChatImage: Navigating Long-Form LLM Answers through Interactive Images](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05290)
*Wencan Jiang,Jiangning Zhang,Yong Liu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: ChatImage将长篇LLM答案转化为可交互的可视化图像，通过结构化模块化布局、渲染与二次视觉落地，对图像中可交互区域叠加热点，实现局部细读与区域化追问，提升可导航性与一致性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 长篇线性文本难以细粒度检查、导航与回访；需要把复杂答案转为直观、可交互的视觉形式，并确保交互区域与可视内容严格对齐。

Method: 1) 将文本答案归一化为结构化视觉模块并规划布局后渲染成图像；2) 使用视觉落地模型（如LocateAnything、MiMo-Vision）对渲染图进行二次落地，必要时用SAM风格掩码细化；3) 根据落地结果在图像上叠加透明可点击热点；4) 每个热点开启细节面板与区域范围的后续对话；5) 将规划坐标作为先验而非最终几何，渲染后再落地以提升点击区域与视觉内容一致性；6) 发布参考实现与含信息图、地图、场景三类格式的30问基准。

Result: 外部模型配置下的评估报告了交互循环完成率、严格的视觉对齐门控指标，以及基于SAM的掩码完整性诊断，显示系统在对齐与交互可用性方面具有可衡量表现。

Conclusion: 将LLM长答案转化为可交互图像并在渲染后再进行视觉落地，可显著改善细粒度浏览与区域化追问的一致性与体验；参考实现与基准为后续研究与比较提供了基础。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) can produce detailed answers to complex queries, but these answers are typically presented as dense linear text, which makes fine-grained inspection, navigation, and return visits difficult. We present ChatImage, a system that converts long-form LLM answers into interactive visual images. Given a textual answer, ChatImage first normalizes its content into structured visual modules, plans a visual layout, and renders a coherent image. It then applies a second grounding pass to the rendered image with vision grounding models such as LocateAnything and MiMo-Vision, with optional SAM-style mask refinement, to identify the visible regions that should support interaction. From these grounded regions, ChatImage overlays transparent clickable hotspots on the image. Each hotspot opens a detail panel and a region-scoped follow-up thread, allowing the user to inspect and query a specific part of the answer without re-reading the full response. Instead of treating planned coordinates as the final interaction geometry, ChatImage uses them as priors and grounds the interaction targets after rendering, which improves consistency between visual content and clickable regions. We release a reference implementation and introduce a 30-question benchmark covering infographic, map, and scene-based answer formats. Evaluation with configured external models reports interaction-loop completion, a strict visual-alignment gate, and a SAM-based mask-completeness diagnostic.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Automated detection of intracranial aneurysms (IAs) from CT angiography (CTA) is severely hindered by high false-positive rates. Convolutional neural networks (CNNs) rely on local pixel intensities, causing systematic confusion between saccular aneurysms and vascular bifurcations -- a problem especially acute for small lesions (<3 mm), where detection sensitivity falls below 60%. We propose a plug-and-play, topology-aware false-positive reduction framework evaluating the Smooth Euler Characteristic Transform (SECT) -- a directional representation encoding global 3D vascular geometry independently of intensity -- against persistence-based summaries (Persistence Images and Landscapes), tested on a stratified subset of the RSNA 2025 dataset. SECT achieves an AUC of 0.943, substantially outperforming direction-agnostic methods (AUC ~0.68), and exhibits a clinical performance inversion: it excels on the sub-3 mm cohort, maintaining 0.943 AUC and 78.5% sensitivity at 95% specificity. The representation is also scanner-agnostic, achieving 0.927 mean AUC under leave-one-scanner-out (LOGO) validation across four manufacturers. By capturing asymmetric geometric invariants rather than intensity profiles, SECT reliably resolves the primary structural confounder in IA detection, positioning it as a robust downstream filter for hybrid deep-learning diagnostic pipelines.

### [312] [Steering Optimisation Trajectories in Diffusion Representation Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05319)
*Rajat Rasal,Avinash Kori,Tian Xia,Ben Glocker*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 论文研究扩散自编码器在图像质量相近时却学到差异巨大的潜在结构，发现源于早期训练的优化动力学存在两种轨迹：重建导向与解缠导向。作者提出通过引导U-Net捷径与控制早期噪声暴露来调节重建-解缠权衡，并据此提出SteeringDRL（门控残差U-Net+噪声曝光课程），在多种解缠与物体中心学习任务上提升表征并降低随机种子敏感性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管扩散自编码器能产生高质量图像，但其潜在表示的“可解缠/可分离性”差异巨大且不稳定；缺乏对这种差异成因及可控性的系统理解与方法。

Method: 1) 分析训练早期的重建质量与潜在表示质量曲线，识别两类稳定优化轨迹（重建优先与解缠渐进）；2) 假设并验证通过干预扩散U-Net中的捷径通路与早期噪声暴露，可塑造上述权衡；3) 提出SteeringDRL：采用门控残差U-Net以抑制捷径、并引入简单的噪声级别曝光课程以引导训练。

Result: 在多种解缠基准上，SteeringDRL提升表示质量、降低对随机种子的敏感性；在物体中心学习中扩展至空间解缠，提升合成和真实数据的分割质量。

Conclusion: 扩散自编码器的潜在结构差异主要来自早期优化动力学与网络捷径/噪声暴露的交互。通过结构门控与噪声课程可系统性地引导训练，实现更强、更稳定的表示与更好的空间解缠。

Abstract: We study why diffusion autoencoders can achieve similar image quality while learning substantially different latent structures. We trace this behaviour to optimisation dynamics; we analyse curves of image reconstruction against latent representation quality, revealing trajectories that organise around two distinct regimes early in training. Models in the reconstruction regime prioritise image fidelity early, whereas those in the disentanglement regime improve reconstruction and disentanglement more gradually. We hypothesise that this behaviour can be influenced by targeting shortcut pathways in the diffusion U-Net and controlling early noise-level exposure, thereby shaping the reconstruction-disentanglement trade-off during training. To steer optimisation toward stronger representations, we introduce SteeringDRL, combining gated residual U-Nets with a simple noise-level exposure curriculum for training. Across disentanglement benchmarks, SteeringDRL improves representation quality and reduces seed sensitivity. Our method further extends to spatial disentanglement in object-centric learning, improving segmentation quality on synthetic and real-world datasets.

We propose CenSynCMB, a centre-guided and mimic-aware framework combining a 3D Attention U-Net, auxiliary centre-map supervision, false-negative-driven reweighting, and fold-wise physics-guided synthesis of positive CMBs and labelled hard negatives.   <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: While feedforward 3D reconstruction excels at efficient novel view synthesis, it typically falters when faced with scenes under varying illumination. To this end, we introduce WildSplat, the first feedforward 3D Gaussian Splatting framework capable of appearance-conditioned novel-view synthesis for unposed in-the-wild images. To handle inconsistent photometric conditions, we propose a dual-branch architecture that explicitly decouples geometry from appearance. The geometry branch extracts an appearance-invariant 3D structure and jointly predicts camera poses. To govern the rendering appearance, the appearance branch injects target appearance cues into the content features via a globally pre-modulated cross-attention mechanism. To further prevent feature entanglement, we introduce a joint multi-reference training strategy that stabilizes the training process. Extensive experiments show that WildSplat surpasses existing optimization-based and feedforward methods, achieving state-of-the-art performance in in-the-wild novel view synthesis and appearance editing from sparse inputs in a single forward pass.

We propose RelGraphOV, a relationship-aware framework that uses 3D scene graphs to enhance open-vocabulary 3D understanding. To aggregate relational context while avoiding feature interference, we introduce an Adaptive Gated Dual-Stream Contextual GAT that separates dense geometric features and semantic CLIP embeddings, performs edge-guided message passing, and adaptively fuses complementary semantics. ### [316] [Multiplayer Interactive World Models with Representation Autoencoders](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05352)
*Anthony Hu,Václav Volhejn,Adrien Ramanana Rahary,Chris Mulder,Aditya Makkar,Amélie Royer,Manu Orsini,Alyx Liao,Adam Jelley,Eloi Alonso,Florian Laurent,Fredrik Norén,James Swingos,Jan Hünermann,Kent Rollins,Lucas Hosseini,Matthieu Le Cauchois,Maxim Peter,Pim de Witte,Tim Brown,Vincent Micheli,Moritz Böhle,Gabriel de Marmiesse,Viktoriia Sharmanska,Lucia Specia,Michael Black,Patrick Pérez*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出首个面向高动态、复杂物理交互环境的多玩家世界模型，在Rocket League中以多智能体动作条件生成稳定长时视频滚动，5B参数、单卡B200实时20FPS。发布数据集、代码与在线演示。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 单玩家世界模型将其他体当作环境，难以归因和在任意多玩家动作组合下保持一致性；需要能理解多体物理与策略交互的生成模型，以支持可扩展、稳定、长时预测与控制研究。

Method: 基于潜变量扩散的5B参数视频生成模型：以多智能体动作流进行条件化，学习将场景变化正确归因到对应玩家；在Rocket League上训练，使用10,000小时公开bot对局数据；系统比较视频编解码、生成目标（扩散/其他）与多玩家条件方案；构建针对物理理解的评测；研究模型与数据规模对能力与失败模式的影响。

Result: 模型可在单张Nvidia B200上实时生成四人比赛20 FPS；尽管仅用短片段训练，推理滚动在分布质量上可稳定至5分钟（观测可持续数小时无崩溃）；展示随着规模提升的能力涌现与残留失败模式；给出有针对性的物理理解评测指标。

Conclusion: 多玩家条件的潜变量扩散世界模型能在复杂物理与紧耦合交互下实现稳定长时视频生成与归因一致性；提供数据、代码与演示以促进多玩家世界模型研究，并为未来在控制、对策与物理理解上的应用奠定基础。

Abstract: We introduce the first multiplayer world model for highly dynamic environments governed by complex physical interactions. Whereas single-player world models treat the other agents as part of the environment, ours conditions on the action streams of multiple agents, learning to attribute changes in the scene to the correct player and to stay coherent under arbitrary combinations of their actions. We study this problem in the game of Rocket League, where players compete and cooperate under fast, tightly coupled dynamics. Trained on 10,000 hours of gameplay collected with publicly available bots, our 5-billion-parameter latent diffusion model generates four-player matches in real time, producing 20 frames per second on a single Nvidia B200 GPU. Although trained only on short clips, its rollouts stay stable far beyond the training horizon: distributional quality holds steady out to five minutes, the longest horizon we measure, and in practice we observe rollouts continuing for hours with no sign of collapse. We systematically investigate the central design choices: the video codec, the generative objective, and the multiplayer conditioning scheme. In addition, we characterize how behavior changes with model and data scale, including the capabilities that emerge and the failure modes that persist. We further develop targeted evaluations that probe the model's physical understanding rather than visual appearance alone. To support continued research on multiplayer world models, we release our dataset, our full training and inference codebase, and a live demo.

### [317] [Geometric Reciprocity: Unlocking Self-Supervision for Stereoscopic Video Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05354)
*Jingyi Lu,Kai Han*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出首个仅用单目视频自监督训练的单目转双目方法，基于几何互易定理（GRT）在最近邻DIBR下可解析计算遮挡/反遮挡掩码，实现训练-测试一致并显著优于无训练与监督SOTA。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: DIBR单目转双目中，视差导致的遮挡空洞需立体修复成为质量瓶颈；现有高质方法依赖稀缺立体数据或有域差的合成数据，限制泛化与规模。

Method: 提出自监督循环一致框架，从单目视频学习；关键为几何互易定理：在最近邻DIBR下，从源到目标的去遮挡掩码等于从目标反向回源时丢失像素的掩码，从而可在测试时仅凭单目图像解析得到遮挡掩码；该一致性使训练与测试的形变/掩码完全对齐，稳定自监督学习。

Result: 在无需立体对的前提下，方法在多基准上显著优于无训练与有监督最新方法；可从海量单目视频学习，减少域差影响。

Conclusion: 通过GRT实现掩码的解析与训练-测试一致的自监督DIBR框架，解决数据匮乏与域差问题，提升单目转双目的质量与泛化能力。

Abstract: Monocular-to-stereo conversion synthesizes stereoscopic content from 2D videos for immersive 3D experiences. In modern Depth-Image-Based Rendering (DIBR) approaches, stereo inpainting of disocclusions is the critical bottleneck. Training-based methods achieve superior quality but rely on scarce stereo pairs or synthetic data with domain gaps. We address this through the first self-supervised framework learning from monocular videos via cycle consistency. Our key contribution is the Geometric Reciprocity Theorem (GRT): under the nearest-neighbor DIBR formulation, the disocclusion mask when synthesizing a target view equals the mask of pixels lost when warping back from target to source, enabling analytical computation of test-time disocclusion masks directly from monocular images. This yields train-test consistency for the stated warping formulation, supporting self-supervised learning from unlimited monocular videos and substantial improvements over training-free and supervised state-of-the-art methods. Project page: https://visual-ai.github.io/grt/

</details>


### [318] [ReCal3R: Reliability-Calibrated Learning Rates for Streaming 3D Reconstruction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05356)
*Xinze Li,Yiyuan Wang,Pengxu Chen,Wentao Fan,Weifeng Su,Weisi Lin,Wentao Cheng*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: ReCal3R提出一种基于可靠度校准的逐token学习率，用于流式三维重建中的循环场景状态更新，显著减轻长序列中状态腐化，提升位姿、深度与重建质量（ATE降至原来的约1/3），且几乎不增加算力开销。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 流式3D重建需在有限内存与线性时间下处理长视频，依赖可复用的循环场景状态。但反复更新易把历史可靠信息被噪声/歧义新观测覆盖，导致“状态漂移/腐化”。需要一种能按可靠度自适应控制更新强度的方法，以在适应新帧与保留已知可靠信息之间取得平衡。

Method: 提出ReCal3R：对每个状态token估计其可靠度，并用以校准候选学习率。候选学习率由三信号推导：token对齐度、状态重建残差、近期更新压力。最终逐token学习率在保守基准率与候选率间插值：对不可靠token抑制激进更新；对信息量高帧保持快速适应。作为训练-Free的校准规则集成到CUT3R中。

Result: 在长序列上显著提升位姿、深度与重建质量，报告ATE约3.7×降低，同时运行时间与内存占用与基线相当。代码已开源。

Conclusion: 可靠度校准的逐token学习率能有效避免循环场景状态在长序列中的腐化，实现稳健的流式3D重建；方法通用、训练无关、代价低，可作为现有循环重建器的即插即用组件。

Abstract: Streaming 3D reconstruction relies on a compact recurrent scene state to process long image streams in linear time and bounded memory. However, repeated updates can gradually corrupt this state, causing reliable historical information to be overwritten by noisy or ambiguous observations. We introduce ReCal3R, a reliability-calibrated learning rate method for recurrent 3D reconstruction. Instead of directly applying a candidate learning rate, our method estimates state token reliability from the maintained scene state and uses it to calibrate a candidate learning rate derived from token alignment, state reconstruction residual, and recent update pressure. The resulting token-wise learning rate interpolates between a conservative base rate and the candidate rate, suppressing aggressive updates on unreliable tokens while preserving adaptation to informative frames. Applied to CUT3R as a training-free calibration rule, ReCal3R reaches strong performance on long sequences in pose, depth, and reconstruction quality, including a 3.7$\times$ reduction in ATE, with comparable runtime and memory. Code is available at: https://github.com/Powertony102/ReCal3R.

</details>


### [319] [PixWorld: Unifying 3D Scene Generation and Reconstruction in Pixel Space](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05373)
*Sensen Gao,Zhaoqing Wang,Qihang Cao,Dongdong Yu,Changhu Wang,Jia-Wang Bian*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出PixWorld：在像素空间用扩散统一3D重建与生成，直接以渲染图监督并引入几何感知损失，优于潜空间方法并达SOTA重建表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法将3D重建（像素回归）与3D生成（潜变量扩散）分离；统一到潜空间会带来：1) 扩散目标不直接作用于真实3D表示；2) VAE/RAE编码造成信息损失；3) 需预训练自编码器，带来依赖与误差累积。需要一种在像素域统一两任务、对3D几何更敏感且避免潜空间瓶颈的方法。

Method: 提出Pixel-space diffusion框架PixWorld：以渲染视图为扩散监督目标，绕过潜编码器，直接对像素域进行扩散优化以对齐3D场景保真度；除常规光度与感知损失外，引入“几何感知损失”，借助预训练3D基础模型的几何感知特征，将渲染视图与真值在几何特征空间对齐，提供3D结构监督；单一模型同时训练/推理完成重建与生成。

Result: PixWorld在3D生成上稳定优于潜空间扩散方法；在3D重建上达到与当前SOTA相当的性能，显示像素域统一方案的有效性与鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 像素空间的统一扩散范式可同时兼顾3D重建与生成，避免潜空间信息损失与外部自编码器依赖；结合几何感知监督可提升3D结构一致性，带来更高保真与更强泛化。

Abstract: 3D reconstruction and generation are commonly tackled by separate paradigms: pixel-based regression for reconstruction, and latent diffusion for generation. Recent works attempt to unify them in latent space, but with notable drawbacks: the diffusion objective is defined on latent features rather than the underlying 3D representation, and both branches suffer from information loss introduced by latent encoding, while requiring a pretrained Variational Autoencoder (VAE) or Representation Autoencoder (RAE). In this paper, we reformulate these two tasks under a unified pixel-space diffusion paradigm and introduce PixWorld, a single model that jointly addresses 3D reconstruction and generation. By supervising diffusion directly on rendered images, PixWorld removes the above limitations and aligns optimization with 3D scene fidelity. Beyond photometric and perceptual supervision that operates at the 2D image level and lacks 3D geometric awareness, we further introduce a geometry perception loss that aligns rendered views with their ground truth in the geometry-aware feature space of a pretrained 3D foundation model, providing 3D structural supervision. PixWorld consistently outperforms prior latent-space generation methods and matches state-of-the-art reconstruction methods, demonstrating the superiority of a unified pixel-space approach.

### [320] [MV-Forcing: Long Multi-View Video Generation via 4D-Grounded Spatio-Temporal Self-Forcing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05376)
*Gal Fiebelman,Hadar Averbuch-Elor,Sagie Benaim*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出MV-Forcing：把时间与多视角自回归统一到一个扩散学生模型中，用3D重建作为视角间的几何桥，支持任意长、多视角的一致动态视频生成。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法要么能生成长时单视角视频（时间自回归），要么能在短时间范围内做多视角一致生成（双向注意力），无法同时做到“长时+多视角一致”的动态场景视频。需要一种既扩展时间长度又保持跨视角几何一致性的框架。

Method: 1) 单一扩散模型内组合时间与视角自回归；2) 在连续视角间插入“4D几何桥”：对已生成源视角进行自回归3D重建（几何与运动），渲染出下一个目标视角的几何先验，再由扩散模型细化成高质量视频；3) 训练期引入联合去噪：两个视角槽同时从噪声初始化，突破教师模型固定时间窗，实现无限时间扩展；4) 采用Distribution Matching Distillation并提出时空Self-Forcing，减小训练-推理暴露偏差，兼顾时间与视角的序列自回归。

Result: 在合成与真实数据上，能生成任意长度与视角数量的动态场景视频，保持多视角几何一致，且用少步学生模型高效推理，优于现有方法。

Conclusion: 通过几何桥接与联合去噪的自回归扩散蒸馏，MV-Forcing实现了长时、多视角一致的动态视频生成，关闭了时空与视角自回归的暴露偏差，提供高效、可扩展的单模型解决方案。

Abstract: Recent advances in video diffusion models have enabled either long single-view generation through temporal autoregression, or short multi-view synthesis through bidirectional attention. However, generating long, multi-view consistent videos of dynamic scenes remains unsolved. In this work, we present MV-Forcing, a framework that composes temporal and view-wise autoregression within a single diffusion model by introducing a 4D geometric bridge between sequentially generated views. Our key insight is that an autoregressive 3D reconstruction model naturally interfaces between autoregressively generated views. Given a completed source view, we reconstruct its 3D structure and render a geometric prior of the next target viewpoint, which the diffusion model refines into a high-quality video. To extend generation beyond the teacher's fixed temporal window, we introduce a joint denoising regime where both view slots are initialized from noise during training, enabling temporally unbounded generation. We distill the model via Distribution Matching Distillation with Spatio-Temporal Self-Forcing, closing the train-inference exposure bias gap for both temporal and view-sequential autoregression. Extensive experiments on both synthetic and real-world data demonstrate that MV-Forcing produces geometrically consistent multi-view videos of dynamic scenes at arbitrary lengths and viewpoint counts using a single few-step student model.

### [321] [Search Beyond What Can Be Taught: Evolving the Knowledge Boundary in Agentic Visual Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05382)
*Haozhe Wang,Weijia Feng,Jinpeng Yu,Che Liu,Ping Nie,Fangzhen Lin,Jiaming Liu,Ruihua Huang,Jimmy Lin,Wenhu Chen,Cong Wei*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 论文提出SearchGen数据与基准，揭示现有视觉生成模型在开放世界知识请求上的严重失效（仅得分21–28/100），并提出“教-后-搜”的共训练框架以学习模型的知识边界、用检索补齐外部知识，从而实现稳健、可递归自改进的工具增强式视觉生成。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 视觉生成模型训练于封闭语料，但用户请求与世界知识是开放且长尾的（新人物、热点实体、截断后事件等），导致模型自信编造；现有基准难以暴露这类失效，需要一个能系统评测“世界知识落差”的基准与方法。

Method: 1) 构建SearchGen-20K与SearchGen-Bench：覆盖12类失败类型、22个领域的20,839条提示，并配套预执行的多模态检索语料SearchGen-Corpus-1M以离线复现。2) 评测前沿开源生成器，揭示大幅性能塌陷。3) 提出“教-后-搜”（teach-then-search）共训练：先教模型识别/内化可学知识，再对剩余超出其能力边界的需求进行有针对性的检索；通过探索并利用“生成器特定、动态演化的知识边界”来避免天真检索带来的噪声注入。

Result: 在SearchGen-Bench上，前沿开源视觉生成器仅得21–28/100，较现有基准低约40分；采用最简版共训练配方即可带来单调提升，检索噪声显著减少，生成更符合世界知识请求。

Conclusion: 视觉生成的核心瓶颈是训练内化知识与开放世界知识之间的结构性缺口。该缺口可通过识别模型知识边界并进行“教-后-搜”共训练来弥合，从而实现面向现实世界知识的、可递归自改进的代理式视觉生成；论文发布完整数据与可回放工具链以促进可复现研究。

Abstract: Visual generators excel at rendering, but they confidently fabricate what they do not know. User requests are unbounded, evolving, and deeply long-tailed: new characters, trending entities, post-cutoff events, and more. This world-knowledge bottleneck is structural: generators are trained on fixed corpora, but the visual world is open-ended. We construct SearchGen-20K and SearchGen-Bench, with 20,839 prompts spanning twelve failure categories and twenty-two domains, paired with a pre-executed multimodal SearchGen-Corpus-1M to support offline, reproducible research. On SearchGen-Bench, frontier open generators score only 21 to 28 out of 100, a 40-point collapse invisible to existing benchmarks. The natural remedy is to employ search tools, enabling agentic visual generation. However, we find that naive search fails: it retrieves indiscriminately, injecting noise into prompts the generator already handles. We trace the root cause to a generator-specific, evolving knowledge boundary: the divide between what a generator can internalize through training and what must remain in external context. Although this boundary is hard to specify in advance, we show that it is discoverable through a teach-then-search co-training framework. Even a minimal version of this co-training recipe produces monotonic improvement, laying the foundation for recursive self-improvement in visual generation that can meet world-knowledge-grounded requests. We release the full dataset, co-training corpus, and search corpus as a replayable harness for tool-augmented, world-knowledge-grounded visual generation.

### [322] [InFlux++: Real and Synthetic Data for Estimating Dynamic Camera Intrinsics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05389)
*Erich Liang,Caleb Kha-Uong,Chinmaya Saran,Sreemanti Dey,David W. Liu,Junhan Ouyang,Benjamin Zhou,Jia Deng*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 论文提出InFlux++：包含大规模合成数据集与更丰富的真实基准，用于视频逐帧相机内参（尤其焦距）估计，显著提升在真实与既有基准上的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现实视频常存在动态内参（变焦、对焦、畸变等），而多数3D方法假设内参固定，导致鲁棒性差。现有方法训练数据稀缺、内参多样性不足；基准也缺少场景/相机运动多样性，难以公平评测。

Method: 构建双组件数据资源：1) InFlux++ Synth：程序化生成的高分辨率视频，441K+标注帧，提供逐帧真实内参，部分还有位姿、深度、法线；包含变焦/变焦距、对焦变化、镜头畸变、景深虚化、动态物体与真实感渲染。2) InFlux++ Real：扩展的真实世界基准，334段高分辨率视频、514K+新帧，场景与相机运动更广。用合成数据微调现有内参预测模型并在真实集上评测。

Result: 在InFlux++ Synth上微调后，现有RGB内参预测方法在InFlux++ Real与原InFlux上均显著提升，特别是焦距估计更准确与稳定。

Conclusion: 大规模、内参多样化的合成监督对逐帧内参预测有效；新基准更全面评测动态内参场景。InFlux++推动RGB视频动态内参估计研究，资源与排行榜公开可用。

Abstract: Camera intrinsics are vital for recovering 3D structure from 2D video. However, most 3D algorithms assume fixed intrinsics throughout a video, an assumption that often fails for real-world in-the-wild videos. Consequently, estimating per-frame intrinsics from RGB images is critical for making 3D methods robust to videos with dynamic intrinsics. InFlux previously advanced this research direction by establishing the first real-world benchmark with per-frame ground truth intrinsics for dynamic intrinsics videos. Nevertheless, existing methods remain inaccurate due to two obstacles: (i) training data is scarce and lacks intrinsics diversity; and (ii) benchmarks, including InFlux, have limited scene and camera motion diversity, making it difficult to properly evaluate methods. To address both gaps, we present InFlux++, consisting of two components. InFlux++ Synth is a large-scale procedurally generated synthetic video dataset with 441K+ annotated frames from 1841 high-resolution videos, providing accurate per-frame ground truth intrinsics for training dynamic intrinsics prediction models; a subset also includes per-frame pose, depth, and normals. The videos feature rich intrinsics diversity through changes in camera zoom and focus, as well as dynamic objects and realistic rendering effects such as lens distortion and defocus blur. InFlux++ Real is a large-scale real-world benchmark that extends InFlux with 514K+ newly captured frames across 334 high-resolution videos, spanning a wider range of scenes and camera motions. Finetuning existing intrinsics prediction methods on InFlux++ Synth consistently improves focal length estimation across both InFlux++ Real and InFlux, suggesting that synthetic supervision is promising for RGB-based intrinsics prediction. For the dataset, benchmark, code, videos, submission instructions, and live leaderboard, please visit https://influx.cs.princeton.edu/ .

### [323] [SynCity 3000: Bootstrapping Scene-Scale 3D Diffusion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05392)
*Paul Engstler,Iro Laina,Christian Rupprecht,Andrea Vedaldi*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: SynCity 3000 提出一种将图像到3D生成器适配为“卷积式”算子的方法，以从单张提示生成的大尺度二测视图出发，生成任意大小、全局一致且细粒度可控的3D场景；通过合成数据引擎微调模型，缓解真实3D场景数据稀缺问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有图像到3D方法可生成单体复杂资产，但难以扩展到大尺度场景，且缺乏全局一致性与布局可控性。同时训练大场景生成需要大量标注/重建的3D场景数据，现实中稀缺。

Method: 1) 设计合成数据引擎，批量生成“类场景”数据以微调现有image-to-3D生成器；2) 将生成器重构/适配为可在空间上滑动的卷积式算子；3) 先由用户文本提示生成整个场景的二测（dimetric）图；4) 对该图施加卷积式3D生成以拼接出全场景，支持任意大小与细粒度布局控制。

Result: 在多样化提示与布局设置下，可生成大规模、细节丰富且全球一致的3D场景，优于以往3D场景生成在连贯性和控制性方面的表现。

Conclusion: 通过卷积化的image-to-3D生成器与合成数据微调，SynCity 3000实现从文本与布局提示到任意尺度、连贯、可控的3D场景生成，缓解数据稀缺并提升场景级生成质量。

Abstract: We present SynCity 3000, a framework for generating 3D scenes that are globally coherent while enabling fine-grained layout control. Building on the ability of current image-to-3D generators to produce complex 3D assets from a single image, we extend this capability to the scale of entire scenes by adapting the generator to be applicable as a convolutional operator. We achieve this by fine-tuning the model on scene-like data generated by a new synthetic data engine, which we propose to address the scarcity of 3D scene data for training. The convolutional generator is then applied to a dimetric image of the entire scene, generated from the user prompt, resulting in 3D scenes of arbitrary size and complexity. Across diverse prompts and layouts, SynCity 3000 produces large, coherent, and detailed scenes, addressing the shortcomings of prior approaches to 3D scene generation.

</details>


### [324] [From Fixed to Free Cameras: Calibration-Free View-Robust Vision-Language-Action Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05396)
*Wenhao Li,Xueying Jiang,Quanhao Qian,Deli Zhao,Shijian Lu,Gongjie Zhang,Ran Xu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: CamVLA提出一种无需外参标定、仅用单目RGB与指令即可在多视角下稳健执行操作的VLA。其核心是把动作预测拆分为相机坐标系下的末端执行器动作与相机到机器人基座的6DoF手眼矩阵，再通过几何变换合成基座系动作，从而显著提升跨视角成功率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现实部署中相机位置/姿态常变化，现有VLA若不显式提供相机外参则鲁棒性差、使用成本高。作者主张策略应自我推断相机几何而非依赖外参输入，以提升易用性与跨视角泛化。

Method: 提出Camera-Centric VLA：
- 预测两部分：(1) 相机坐标系下的末端执行器动作；(2) 相机到机器人基座的6DoF手眼矩阵。
- 通过确定性的几何变换将两者组合为基座系动作，实现“动作生成”与“几何定位”的解耦。
- 无需深度、无需外参标定、单目单视角输入（RGB+指令）。

Result: 在仿真与真实机器人数据上，CamVLA在未见过的多种视角下稳定提高任务成功率，相比基线更鲁棒。项目页提供更多细节与可视化。

Conclusion: 通过相机中心动作表示与手眼估计的联合预测，CamVLA实现了无需外参的跨视角稳健操控，降低部署成本并提升实用性。

Abstract: Real-world robot deployment rarely maintains the training-stage camera setup, where cameras often experience repositioning or remounting depending on actual scenarios. Existing view-robust Vision-Language-Action (VLA) policies tolerate such camera variations only when the camera extrinsics are explicitly provided, making them fragile and hard to use especially when view robustness is critical. We argue that the policy should not be told where the camera is, but rather figure it out by itself. To this end, we introduce Camera-Centric VLA (CamVLA), a new VLA model that decouples manipulation controls from camera geometry by predicting (i) a camera-centric end-effector action expressed in the local camera frame, and (ii) a 6-DoF hand-eye matrix relating cameras to the robot base. A deterministic geometric transformation composes the two predictions into a robot base-frame action. This disentangles how I should move in pose-independent camera-centric action generation from where I am looking from in camera-perspective geometric grounding. The resulting policy is calibration-free, depth-free, and single-view, requiring only a single monocular RGB image as the visual observation and task instruction at deployment. Evaluations in both simulation and real-world robot data show that CamVLA consistently improves success rates across diverse unseen viewpoints. Project page: https://alibaba-damo-academy.github.io/CamVLA/.

</details>
